 When I think of Ichijou's condition, my heart becomes very complicated.　The shiver of horror at the apparent severity of the injury, the fear and trepidation at the prospect of the girl's death, the relief at the fact that she was recovering, and the unshakeable doubt about that fact. doubts.

I'm no longer a scarecrow with a great title and no substance.　I've become someone who can proudly say that I'm fighting for what's right.

With my own hands, I've defeated evil!　There's only one. One big one. I'm sure that as long as that monk is in charge of this world, he will continue to make more people like Okabe's princess suffer.

ようやく父の教えに恥じない娘になれたように思う。　父様は言った。悪を憎め、認めるな、決して許してはならないと。
I think I have finally become a daughter who is not ashamed of her father's teachings.　My father said. Hate evil, do not admit it, and never forgive it.

正義とは、人として正しい在り方。人の原則。正道。　邪悪とは、それに背くことを云う。人の逸脱。外道。
Justice is the right way to be as a person. The principles of humanity. The right way.　Wickedness is to go against it. The deviation of a person. Outer path.

悪を滅ぼしてこそ、世は正しく導かれる。　だから命に懸けて否定する。否定して戦う。戦って滅ぼす。
Only by destroying evil can the world be led righteously.　That's why I risk my life to deny it. Deny it and fight it. Fight and destroy.

例えその悪にやむなき理由があろうと、見逃してはならない。〝必要悪〟を認めてはならない。これを許す限り悪は絶対に滅びない。
Do not overlook evil, even if there is a compelling reason for it. We must not allow "necessary evil. As long as we allow this, evil will never be destroyed.

正義が邪悪に勝利する日は来ない。　悪の犠牲になる人も絶えない。
The day will never come when justice will triumph over evil.　There will always be people who fall victim to evil.

――滅ぼすのだ。　悪はすべて。理由を問わず。一切。
--Destroy it.　All evil. No matter the reason. All of them.

わけてもあの Yusa Doushinのように、悪のため悪を行う奴輩は。　人の世界から追い出して相応の地獄へ突き落とすに如かず、だ。
Especially those who do evil for evil's sake, like that Yusa Doushin.　It is better to drive them out of the human world and throw them into the hell they deserve.

父様はきっと褒めてくれる。　よくやったって言ってくれる。
I'm sure your father will praise me.　He'll tell me I did well.

興奮し過ぎて、頭に血が昇ったみたいだ。　軽い眩暈。あたしは額を押さえた。
I think I got overexcited and the blood rushed to my head.　I felt light-headed. I held my forehead.

……少し、熱いような気がする。　もしかすると微熱があるのかもしれない。
...... I feel a little, hot.　Maybe you have a slight fever.

ここまで回復しておいて、明日からは風邪で改めて寝込み、なんて御免だ。　後で泣きを見ないためには、用心して休んでおいた方がいい。 Minato-sanにも無理は厳禁と言われているし。
After recovering so well, I don't want to have to go back to bed tomorrow with a cold.　It's better to be cautious and take a rest so that I won't be crying later. Minato-san also told me not to overdo it.

これは悪を憎む力だ。　強力を振るって力弱き人々を苦しめる、そんな自惚れた奴輩を、更に上回る暴威でもって叩き潰してやるための力なのだ。
This is the power to hate evil.　It is the power to crush with even greater violence those who wield power to torment the weak and smug.

まさに正義！　その体現！
Justice!　The embodiment of it!

《如何にも！　ゆけ、 midou!》
How dare you!　Go, midou!

「応！」
"Yes!

悪は今そこにいる。　養母を殺そうとしている山賊の musha！
Evil is out there now.　Bandits trying to kill my adoptive mother musha!

彼はこちらを見て泡を食っている様子だった。　馬鹿め！　自分だけが力の所有者だと思っていたのだろう！
He looked at me and seemed to be foaming at the mouth.　Fool!　He must have thought he was the only one who owned the power!

自分だけが好き放題に暴力で人を害せるのだと信じ込んでいたのだろう！　その傲慢にいま報いをやる。
You were convinced that you were the only one who could harm people with violence at will!　I will now reward you for your arrogance.

悪の暴力は必ず正義の鉄槌の前に散るのだ！
The violence of evil will always fall before the hammer of justice!

《ＤＡＡＡＩＩＡＡＡＡＡＡＡＡＨＨＨＨ!》
DAAIIAAAAAAAAHHHH!

敵は養母に向かって太刀を振り下ろしている。　だが、それが届く前に、
The enemy is swinging his sword at my foster mother.　But before it could reach her.

俺が奴を斬り伏せる――――
I'll cut him down. ----

その――――刹那。
That ---- moment.

養母が俺を見たのに気付いた。
I noticed that my foster mother looked at me.

「――――――――」
